    > // å› æ­¤ï¼Œ NaN ==  NaN ä¼šåˆ¤æ–­æˆ False

    > ```js

        }else{
            num = b;
        }*/
        
        var num = a <=b ? a : b;
        
        // document.write(num);
        for(var i = num; i >= 1;i--){
            if( a % i == 0 && b % i ==0){
                document.write(i + '*');
                break;
            }
        }
        
        
        ```
        
    + ```js
        è¾“å…¥ä¸¤ä¸ªæ•°nå’Œa.
        æ¯”å¦‚ nä¸º3 ï¼Œ a ä¸º2çš„è¯ï¼Œè¾“å‡º 2+22+222
        æ¯”å¦‚ nä¸º4 ï¼Œ a ä¸º3çš„è¯ï¼Œè¾“å‡º 3+33+333+3333çš„å€¼ã€‚
        
        var n = 4;
        var a = 3;
        //output 2 22 222
        // n=1 --2
        // n=2 --22
        // n=3 ---222
        var sum = 0;
        var finalSum = 0;
        for(var i = 0; i <= (n-1); i++){
            sum = a * Math.pow(10,i ) + sum;
            // document.write(sum + '</br>');
            finalSum += sum;
            // document.write(finalSum + '</br>');
        }
        document.write(finalSum);
        ```
    
    + ```js
        äº”ä½æ•°ä¸­ï¼Œå¯¹ç§°çš„æ•°ç§°ä¸ºå›æ–‡æ•°ã€‚æ¯”å¦‚ 12321ï¼Œæ‰¾å‡ºæ‰€æœ‰å›æ–‡æ•°ã€‚
        for(var i = 10000; i <= 99999; i++ ){

                document.write(i+'</br>');
            }
        }
        ```

        ** switché…åˆbreak**

        	var year=parseInt(prompt('è¾“å…¥å¹´'));

            for (var i=1;i<month;i++){

         ///æœˆä»½ æ€»æ•°

         /// 7æœˆ 6

         ///rabbit(4) =  rabbit(3) + rabbit(1);
         ///rabbit(n) =  rabbit(n-1) + rabbit(n-3);

           if(n < 4){
             return 1

        åŠŸèƒ½: ä»å¤´éƒ¨æ’å…¥å…ƒç´

        ```

         

    5. > æ€»ç»“ï¼š å¤´æ’  unshift 
        >
        >  å¤´å– shift
        >
        > å°¾æ’ push
        >

    12. ```js
        sort()æ–¹æ³•

        å¦‚æœè¦ä»å¤§åˆ°å°æ’åºï¼Œé‚£å°±æŠŠæ¯”è¾ƒå‡½æ•°é‡Œçš„aå’Œbåè¿‡æ¥ã€‚

        *************
         sort()å’Œ reverse()ï¼Œä»–ä»¬éƒ½ä¼šæŠŠåŸæ•°ç»„æ”¹å˜ã€‚è€Œä¸”è¿”å›å€¼ä¹Ÿæ˜¯æ”¹å˜åçš„æ–°æ•°ç»„ï¼Œ
        è¿™å°±å¯¼è‡´äº†ï¼Œä»–ä»¬çš„ä¸€ä¸ªå…±åŒç‚¹ï¼Œé‚£å°±æ˜¯ è¿”å›å€¼çš„æ•°ç»„ å’Œ æ”¹å˜ä¹‹å‰çš„æ•°ç»„ï¼Œéƒ½å˜äº†ã€‚

        //  éƒ½æ˜¯å˜åŒ–ä¹‹åçš„æ–°ç”Ÿæˆçš„æ•°ç»„ï¼Œ ä¹Ÿå°±æ˜¯è¯´ï¼Œä¼šæ”¹å˜åŸæ•°ç»„ã€‚
                                                                
        ```

    13. æ•°ç»„æ±‚å¹³å‡æ•°

        > â€‹	é¢˜ç›®ï¼šæœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°ç»„ï¼Œæœ‰30ä¸ªä½ç½®ï¼Œä»ä¸€å·ä½å¼€å§‹ï¼Œåˆ†åˆ«æ˜¯0ï¼Œ2ï¼Œ4ï¼Œ6....ä¸€ç›´åˆ°60.
        >
        > â€‹	ç°åœ¨è¦æ±‚æŠŠè¿™äº›æ•°ï¼Œæ¯äº”ä¸ªä¸€å–ï¼Œç„¶åæŠŠè¿™äº”ä¸ªæ•°æ±‚å¹³å‡æ•°ï¼Œç„¶åæ”¾å…¥åˆ°ä¸€ä¸ªæ–°çš„æ•°ç»„ä¸­ã€‚

        ```js
        function average(){
            var arr1 = new Array(30);
            var arr3 =[];
            for(var i = 0; i < arr1.length; i++){
                arr1[i] = (i + 1) * 2;
            }
            // alert(arr1);
            // document.write(arr1);
            for( var j = 0; j < 6;j++){
                // alert(arr1);
                // alert(arr1.length);
                var arr2 = arr1.splice(0,5);
        
               /* 
               Same
               var arr2 =  arr1.slice( 5 * j , 5 * (j+1)  ); 
               Same
               */
        
                // document.write(arr2 + '</br>');
                // calculate the avarge of each arr2;
                /* 
                if use the arrary.slice( ) , instead of splice();
                arr1.slice(0 , 5);  ---first time ,when j = 0
                arr1.slice(5 , 10); ---second time, when j = 1
                arr1.slice(10,  15);----third time, when j = 2
                ... six times total
        
                var arr2 =  arr1.slice( 5 * j , 5 * (j+1)  );
        
                */
                var sum = 0
                for(var k = 0; k < arr2.length;k++){
                    sum += arr2[k]; 
                }
                // alert(sum);
                // document.write(sum + '</br>');
                var average = sum / arr2.length;
                //document.write(average + '</br>');
                arr3.push(average);
            }
            document.write(arr3);
        
        }
        
        average();
        ```

## Reference data type

1. åŸºæœ¬æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ï¼š Value Data Type

2. é—®é¢˜ï¼š

    ```js

    // num2 --> 20;
    
    è¿™å°±æ˜¯æ­£å¸¸çš„ åŸºæœ¬æ•°æ®ç±»å‹çš„èµ‹å€¼ï¼Œvarä¹‹åå°±æ˜¯ç®€å•çš„ç”³æ˜å˜é‡ï¼Œç„¶åèµ‹å€¼ï¼Œå˜é‡èµ‹å€¼å˜é‡ï¼Œå®è´¨ä¸Šå°±æ˜¯æŠŠå˜é‡é‡Œé¢çš„å€¼æå–å†èµ‹ç»™ä¸‹ä¸€ä¸ªå˜é‡è€Œå·²ã€‚

    ```

3. è€Œä¸” å¼•ç”¨æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ï¼Œæ˜¯ä¸èƒ½æ¯”è¾ƒå¤§å°çš„ã€‚

    ```js
    -åœ¨arrayé‡Œï¼Œå› ä¸º æ•°ç»„é•¿åº¦æ˜¯å˜åŒ–çš„ï¼Œä½†æ˜¯åœ¨å†…å­˜ä¸­ ç”³æ˜ä¸€ä¸ªå˜é‡å¿…é¡»æå‰ç”³æ˜æ‰€å ç©ºé—´å†…å­˜å¤§å°ï¼Œæ˜¯ä¸å¯ä»¥äº‹åå†æ›´æ”¹çš„ï¼Œé‚£å°±å’Œarrayçš„å±æ€§çŸ›ç›¾äº†ï¼Œå› ä¸ºä½ æ•°ç»„é‡Œé¢å‚¨å­˜çš„æ•°æ®æ˜¯æ—¶æ—¶åˆ»åˆ»å‘ç”Ÿå˜åŒ–çš„ã€‚

    -æ‰€ä»¥ï¼Œå½“ä½  æŠŠarr2 èµ‹å€¼ç»™ arr1æ—¶å€™ï¼Œåªæ˜¯æŠŠç¼–å·ä¼ ç»™äº† arr1ï¼Œ ä¸¤è€…æ‰€æŒ‡çš„æŒ‡é’ˆå…¶å®éƒ½æŒ‡å‘åŒä¸€ä¸ª [å †]ã€‚æ‰€ä»¥ ä½ å†æ”¹å˜ä»»ä½• ã€1ï¼Œ2ï¼Œ3ã€‘çš„æ•°æ®çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œå †é‡Œé¢çš„æ•°æ®æ”¹å˜äº†ï¼Œé‚£ä½ ä¸ç®¡æ˜¯arr1è¿˜æ˜¯arr2ï¼ŒæŒ‡å‘éƒ½æ˜¯è¿™ä¸ªã€å †ã€‘ï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥å½“ç„¶å…¨éƒ½å˜åŒ–äº†ã€‚
    
    ```

    

5. å®è·µä¸­çš„è§£å†³åŠæ³•ï¼š

    1. concat() æ¥å¤åˆ¶æ•°ç»„ã€‚

        ```js
        concat æ–¹æ³•ã€‚ å›é¡¾ä¸€ä¸‹ï¼š 
        1. ä¸æ”¹å˜åŸæ•°ç»„ï¼ˆå› ä¸ºæ˜¯å…ˆå¤åˆ¶ä¸€ä¸ªåŸæ•°ç»„çš„åˆ†èº«ï¼Œå†åœ¨åˆ†èº«ä¸Šè¿›è¡Œæ“ä½œçš„ï¼Œä¸”åˆ†èº«æŒ‡å‘å¦ä¸€ä¸ªå †ï¼Œåªæ˜¯2ä¸ªå †é‡Œé¢çš„æ•°æ®ä¸€æ¨¡ä¸€æ ·ç½¢äº†ï¼‰ã€‚
        2. å‚æ•° å¯ä»¥å¡«ä»»æ„ï¼Œä½†æ˜¯ å¦‚æœå¡« æ•°ç»„ï¼Œä»–ä¼šæ‹†åˆ†æˆå­æ•°æ®ï¼Œèåˆè¿›å»
        3. è¿”å›å€¼---èåˆåçš„æ–°æ•°ç»„
        æ‰€ä»¥ï¼š
        var arr1 =[1,2,3];
        var arr2 = arr1.concat();
        arr2.push(4);
        alert(arr1);
        // arr1 ä¸å˜åŒ–,è¿˜æ˜¯ [1,2,3,4]

## å†’æ³¡æ’åº bubbleSort

1. åŸç†ï¼š

    > â€‹	å°±æ˜¯å‰åä¸¤ä¸¤æ¯”è¾ƒï¼Œå¦‚æœå‰é¢çš„ å¤§äº åé¢çš„ï¼Œå°±äº¤æ¢ä½ç½®ã€‚
    >
    >  ä¿è¯ åé¢çš„æ•°ä¸€å®šæ¯”å‰é¢çš„å¤§ï¼Œæ¯ä¸€è½®ï¼Œéƒ½å¯ä»¥æŠŠä¸€ä¸ªæœ€å¤§æ•°æµ®åˆ°æœ€æœ€åã€‚å°±å¯ä»¥å®ç°ä»å°åˆ°å¤§æ’åºäº†ã€‚

    ```js
    æ•°ç»„é•¿åº¦ - å½“å‰æ˜¯ç¬¬ n è½®   =  å½“å‰ç¬¬nè½®çš„æ¯”è¾ƒæ¬¡æ•°ï¼›//å› ä¸ºä¸¤ä¸¤æ¯”è¾ƒï¼Œè€Œä¸”æ¯è½®ä¼šå†»ä½æœ€åä¸€ä¸ªæ•°ï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥æ¯”å¦‚ç¬¬ä¸‰è½®ï¼Œé‚£å·²ç»å†»ä½2ä¸ªæ•°äº†ï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥ è¯¥è½®ä¸‹éœ€è¦æ¯”è¾ƒçš„æ•° åªæœ‰length - 2ä¸ªï¼Œ é‚£length -2ä¸ªï¼Œéœ€è¦æ¯”è¾ƒå‡ æ¬¡å‘¢ï¼Ÿéœ€è¦æ¯”è¾ƒ length -2 -1ä¸ªï¼Œæ¯”å¦‚ 6ä¸ªæ•°ï¼Œç¬¬ä¸‰è½®çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œå°±å‰©4ä¸ªæ•°è¦æ¯”è¾ƒäº†ï¼Œé‚£4ä¸ªæ•°è¦æ¯”è¾ƒå‡ æ¬¡å‘¢ï¼Œç­”æ¡ˆæ˜¯3æ¬¡ã€‚æ‰€ä»¥ ç¬¬ä¸‰è½®ï¼Œè¦æ¯”è¾ƒ3æ¬¡ã€‚ 
    ```

    ```js
    è¦æ¯”è¾ƒå¤šå°‘è½® = æ•°ç»„é•¿åº¦ - 1ï¼› //å› ä¸ºæ¯ä¸€è½®æµ®å‡ºæ¥ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°åˆ°æœ€åã€‚
    ```

    

2. ä¾‹å­ï¼š

    ```js
    åŸæ•°ç»„æ˜¯ var array = [9,8,7];
    ç”¨å†’æ³¡æ’åºå°±æ˜¯ï¼š
    ----
    ç¬¬ä¸€è½®ï¼š 
    9 8 7ï¼ˆåŸå§‹ï¼‰
    8 9 7
    8 7 9 ç»“æŸ
    æ‰€ä»¥æ¯”è¾ƒ2æ¬¡ï¼ŒåŸå§‹ä¸ç®—
    ----
    ç¬¬äºŒè½®
    8  7 ï¼ˆåŸå§‹ï¼‰
    7  8  (ç»“æŸ)
    æ‰€ä»¥æ¯”è¾ƒ1æ¬¡ï¼ŒåŸå§‹ä¸ç®—
    ----
    è¾“å‡ºç»“æœ 7 8 9ã€‚
    ```

3. å®ç°:

    ```js
    function bubbleSort(arr){
        // [9,8,7,6,5,4]
        for(var i = 0;i < (arr.length - 1);i++){
            // å¾ªç¯ arr.length - 1 è½®ï¼› æ¯”å¦‚6ä¸ªé•¿åº¦ï¼Œè¦æ¯”è¾ƒ5æ¬¡ã€‚
            for(var j = 0; j < (arr.length - (i + 1));j++){
                //ç¬¬ï¼ˆi+1ï¼‰è½®æ—¶ï¼Œåœ¨è¯¥è½®ä¸‹è¦ æ‰§è¡Œ length - ï¼ˆi+1) æ¬¡æ¯”è¾ƒï¼›
                // æ¯”å¦‚ï¼š ç¬¬ 1 è½®ï¼ˆi = 0ï¼‰æ—¶ï¼Œè¦åœ¨ç¬¬ 1è½®ä¸‹ï¼Œ æ¯”è¾ƒ 6 - ï¼ˆ 0+1ï¼‰ =5 æ¬¡ã€‚
                //ä¹Ÿå°±æ˜¯è¯´ i =0 æ—¶ï¼Œ j =5 ï¼Œ i =1 æ—¶ï¼Œj =4.
                if (arr[j] > arr[j+1]){
                    var temp = arr[j];
                    arr[j] = arr[j+1];
                    arr[j+1] = temp;
                }
            }
        }
        return arr;
    }
    
    var arr1 = [9,8,7,6,5,4];
    bubbleSort(arr1);
    alert(arr1);
    // var res = bubbleSort([9,8,7,6,5,4]);
    // console.log(res);
    ```

## é€‰æ‹©æ’åºselectionSort

1. é€»è¾‘ï¼š ä»ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªä½ç½®å¼€å§‹ï¼Œä»è¯¥ä½ç½®å¼€å§‹å’Œåé¢æ‰€æœ‰çš„æ•°è¿›è¡Œæ¯”è¾ƒï¼Œä½†æ˜¯å’Œå†’æ³¡æ’åºä¸åŒçš„æ˜¯ï¼Œå®ƒä¸æ˜¯ç›¸é‚»çš„ä¸¤ä¸¤æ¯”è¾ƒè€Œæ˜¯ï¼Œå¾€åæ‰€æœ‰ä½ç½®æ¯”è¾ƒã€‚æ¯”å¦‚1å·ä½ï¼Œä»–æ˜¯1å·ä½å’Œ2å·ä½ï¼Œ1å·ä½å’Œ3å·ä½ï¼Œ1å·ä½å’Œ4å·ä½.... å¦‚æ­¤æ¯”è¾ƒä¸‹å»ã€‚

2. è§„å¾‹ï¼š

    1. > â€‹	æ¯æ¬¡è½®éƒ½èƒ½é€‰å‡ºä¸€ä¸ªæœ€å°çš„åœ¨æœ€å‰é¢ã€‚ç„¶åå¼¹å‡ºã€‚ ä¸‹ä¸€è½®å°‘ä¸€ä¸ªç»§ç»­ã€‚

    2. å…¬å¼ï¼š

        > â€‹	 è¦è¿›è¡Œå‡ è½®    =  æ•°ç»„é•¿åº¦  - 1ï¼›ï¼ˆå› ä¸ºæ¯æ¬¡é€‰å‡ºä¸€ä¸ªã€‚è¿™å’Œå†’æ³¡ä¸€æ ·ï¼‰
        >
        > â€‹	è¯¥è½®ä¸‹è¦æ¯”è¾ƒçš„æ¬¡æ•°  = æ•°ç»„é•¿åº¦ - å½“å‰ç¬¬nè½® ï¼ˆä¹Ÿå’Œå†’æ³¡ä¸€æ ·ï¼‰

    3. å®ç°ï¼š

        ```js
        function selectionSortAsc(arr){
            // var arr = [9,8,7,6,5,4]
            for(var i = 0;i < arr.length -1;i++){
                // i = 0 ,1 ,2, 3, 4,
                // i = 0 ç¬¬ä¸€è½®ï¼Œ æ¯”è¾ƒ 5æ¬¡
                for(var j = i + 1;j < arr.length ;j++){
                    // i = 0, j= i+1 = 1, j å– 1ï¼Œ2ï¼Œ3ï¼Œ4ï¼Œ5.ç¡®å®æ¯”è¾ƒ5æ¬¡ï¼›
                    //å…³é”®æ˜¯è¿™ä¸ª5æ¬¡æ€ä¹ˆæ¯”è¾ƒ;
                    //æ¯”è¾ƒçš„æ—¶å€™æ˜¯ï¼Œ 1å·ä½ å’Œ2å·ä½ï¼Œ 1å·ä½vs3å·ä½ï¼Œ 1å·ä½vs4å·ä½ï¼Œ1å·ä½vs5å·ä½ï¼Œ1å·ä½vs6å·ä½ã€‚
                    //åˆ†åˆ«å¯¹åº”çš„å°±æ˜¯ arr[0] vs arr[1] | arr[0] vs arr[2] |arr[0] vs arr[3] | arr[0] vs arr[4]|arr[0] vs arr[5] ;
                    //æ‰€ä»¥è¯´ï¼Œ arr[0] --> arr[i] ,arr[1] -- arr[5] : arr[j]
                    if( arr[i] > arr[j]){
                        var temp = arr[i];
                        arr[i] = arr[j]    
                        arr[j] = temp;
                    }
                }
        
            }
        
        }
        ```

## æ•°ç»„ç»ƒä¹ 

   1. ```js
      éšæœºç»™å‡ºä¸€ä¸ªäº”ä½ä»¥å†…çš„æ•°ï¼Œç„¶åè¾“å‡ºæœ‰å¤šå°‘ä½ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”æ¯ä½åˆ†åˆ«æ˜¯ä»€ä¹ˆï¼Ÿ
      var num = 12345;
      numCount(num);
      
      function numCount(num){
          var arr = new Array;
          while(num > 0){
              //ä»»ä½•æ•° % 10 éƒ½å¯ä»¥æ±‚åˆ°ä»–çš„ ä¸ªä½æ•°ã€‚
              arr.push(num % 10);
              // æŠŠåŸæ•°é™¤ä»¥10 å†å–æ•´æ•°æ®µã€‚

          }
          document.write('ä¸€å…±æœ‰'+ arr.length+'ä½'+'</br>'+ 'æ¯ä½åˆ†åˆ«æ˜¯' + arr.reverse());
      }
      
      å¦ä¸€ç§ä¸ç”¨arrayçš„æ€è·¯ã€‚
      // var num = 123456;
      // var count = 0;
      // while( num > 0){
      //     var res = num % 10;
      //     document.write('åˆ†åˆ«æ˜¯' + res);
      //     num = parseInt(num / 10);
      //     count++;
          
      // }
      // document.write(count);
      ```

   2. ```js
      ç¼–å†™ä¸€ä¸ªå‡½æ•°has (arr,60)åˆ¤æ–­æ•°ç»„ä¸­æ˜¯å¦å­˜åœ¨60è¿™ä¸ªå…ƒç´ ã€‚è¿”å›å¸ƒå°”ç±»å‹ã€‚
      function has(arr,item){
          for(var i = 0; i < arr.length; i++){
              if(arr[i] === item){
                  return true;
              }
          }
          return false;
      }
      ```

   3. ```js
      å†™ä¸€ä¸ªå‡½æ•°åˆ¤æ–­æ˜¯å¦æ˜¯è´¨æ•°è¿˜æ˜¯åˆæ•°ï¼ˆåˆ©ç”¨returnçš„ç»ˆæ­¢ç‰¹æ€§ï¼‰
      function zhishu(num){
          for(var i = 2; i < num; i++){
              if(num % i == 0){
                  return 'heshi';
              }
          }
          return 'zhishu';
      }

   4. ```js
      å®ç°ä¸€ä¸ªæ¡å½¢ç å‡½æ•° ean().è¾“å…¥12ä½æ¡å½¢ç ï¼Œè¾“å‡ºä¸€ä¸ª13ä½æ¡å½¢ç 
      ä¾‹å¦‚ï¼š ä¸€ä¸ª12ä½ 692223361219. Outputæ˜¯ 6922233612192

      function ean13(num){
          var numchain = num;
          var arr = new Array;
          // extract every number of the code into an array.
          while( num > 0){
              arr.unshift(num % 10);
              num = parseInt(num / 10);
          }
          // document.write(arr);
          // document.write('</br>');
          var arrOdd = new Array;
          var arrEven =new Array;
          for(var i = 0; i <arr.length; i++){
              if(i % 2 === 0){
                  arrEven.push(arr[i]);
              }else{
                  arrOdd.push(arr[i]);
              }
          }
               //document.write(arrEven);
               //document.write('</br>');
               //document.write(arrOdd);
               //document.write('</br>');
          var sumOdd = 0;
          var sumEven = 0;
          for(var j = 0; j < arrOdd.length;j++){
              sumOdd += arrOdd[j];
          }
          for(var k = 0; k < arrEven.length;k++){
              sumEven += arrEven[k];
          }
          //document.write(sumOdd);
          //document.write('</br>');
          //document.write(sumEven);
          //document.write('</br>');
          var num13 =  10 - ( ( sumEven + (sumOdd * 3) ) % 10);
          if(num13 == 10){
              num13 = 0;
          }
          var numchain = (numchain *10) + num13;
         // or we can do like this:
          // arr.push(num13);
          // var numchain = Number( arr.join() );
      
      
          return numchain;
      
      }

## NaN == NaN ä¸ºfalseï¼ŒNaN != NaNä¸ºtrue.

```js
 var haha = (NaN != NaN);
    document.write(haha);
// true;

 var haha = (NaN == NaN);
    document.write(haha);
// false;

//ç‰¹åˆ«è¯¡å¼‚ï¼Œä¸€å®šè¦æ³¨æ„ã€‚
```



```js
æœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªå¦‚ä¸‹éœ€æ±‚ï¼Œåˆ¤æ–­æ•°ç»„ä¸­çš„æ•°æ˜¯å¦å…¨éƒ¨ä¸º æ•°å­—ã€‚


æˆ‘é”™è¯¯çš„æ–¹æ³•ï¼š
    var arr=[1,2,3,'ww'];
    var res = arr.every(function(value,index,arr){
        document.write(Number(value) + '</br>');
        return Number(value) != NaN;
      //return isNaN(value) == false; isNaNä¸ºfalseï¼Œä¸æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªnumberä¸ºå‡ï¼Œé‚£å°±æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªnumberã€‚åˆ¤æ–­ç»“æœreturn falseã€‚

      //ä½ å¦‚æœåˆ¤æ–­ æ‰€æœ‰Number(value)éƒ½ä¸ç­‰äºNaNçš„è¯ã€‚è¡¨é¢ä¸Šæ„æ€æ˜¯å¯¹çš„ï¼Œ every valueéƒ½ä¸ç­‰äº NaN,é‚£ä¸ç­‰äº	NaNï¼Œè‚¯å®šå°±æ˜¯ä¸ªnumberã€‚
      //ä½†æ˜¯å…¶å®æ˜¯é”™çš„ï¼Œ å› ä¸º å­˜åœ¨ NaN != NaN ä¹Ÿä¸ºtrueï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥å°±å¯¼è‡´ å…¨éƒ¨éƒ½ä¸ºtrueã€‚arr.every()åˆ¤æ–­å®Œç»“æœä¸ºtrueï¼Œè¿™æ˜¾ç„¶ä¸å¯¹ã€‚
    });
    alert(res);

æ­£ç¡®åšæ³•ä¸€ï¼š
ç”¨ isNaN(Number)æ¥åˆ¤æ–­,æ³¨æ„ isNaNçš„æ„æ€ ä¸æ˜¯æ•°å­—ã€‚ã€‚
ç¼ºç‚¹ï¼š '3' ä¼šåˆ¤æ–­æˆ falseï¼Œä»–è™½ç„¶æ˜¯stringï¼Œä½†æ˜¯è¿˜æ˜¯çº¯æ•°å­—ã€‚
			'NaN'ä¼šåˆ¤æ–­æˆ trueï¼Œ å› ä¸ºNaNè‚¯å®šä¸æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªnumber
      null ä¼šåˆ¤æ–­ç§° falseï¼Œå› ä¸ºnullæ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªnumber
æ‰€ä»¥ï¼Œè¿™åªæ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªçº¯ç²¹çš„ç”¨æ¥checkæ•°ç»„å…ƒç´ æ˜¯ä¸æ˜¯ ã€çº¯æ•°å­—ã€‘çš„æ–¹æ³•

Number.isNaN(NaN);        // true
Number.isNaN(Number.NaN); // true
Number.isNaN(0 / 0);      // true
isNaN('2005/12/12') //true

// e.g. these would have been true with global isNaN()
Number.isNaN('NaN');      // false
Number.isNaN(undefined);  // false
Number.isNaN({});         // false
Number.isNaN('blabla');   // false

// These all return false
Number.isNaN(true);
Number.isNaN(null);
Number.isNaN(37);
Number.isNaN('37');
Number.isNaN('37.37');
Number.isNaN('');
Number.isNaN(' ');

æ­£ç¡®åšæ³•äºŒï¼š ç”¨æ­£åˆ™è¡¨è¾¾å¼åˆ¤æ–­ã€‚

```

9. ```js
    å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ç›¸å…³ç»ƒä¹ :
    1.  å°†å­—ç¬¦ä¸²  str = 'When i was young ,I love a girl in neighoubr class'ä¸­ æå–yong åˆ°girl ç”Ÿæˆæ–°å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œä½†æ˜¯ä¸å‡†countã€‚
    var str = 'When i was young ,I love a girl in neighoubr class';
    var start =str.indexOf('young');
    var end = str.indexOf('girl') + 'girl'.length;
    //ä½†æ˜¯è¿™ä¸ªåº”ä»˜ä¸äº† girlå¦‚æœå‡ºç°ä¸€ä¸ª åœ¨ youngå‰é¢çš„æƒ…å†µã€‚
    var newStr =str.substring(start,end);
    alert(newStr)
    
    2.å°†å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸­çš„å•è¯ç”¨ç©ºæ ¼åˆ†å¼€
    å·²çŸ¥ä¼ å…¥çš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²åªæœ‰å­—æ¯ï¼Œæ¯ä¸ªå•è¯çš„é¦–å­—æ¯å¤§å†™ã€‚ç°åœ¨è¦æ±‚æŠŠæ¯ä¸ªå•è¯ç”¨ç©ºæ ¼éš”å¼€ï¼Œåªä¿ç•™ä¸€ä¸ªå•è¯çš„é¦–å­—æ¯å¤§å†™ã€‚
    Input : HelloMyWorld
    Output: Hello my world
    
    
    function wordTransfer(str){
        //Input->  HelloMyWorld
        //Output-> Hello my world
        var arr = str.split('');
        arr[0] = arr[0].toUpperCase();
        // alert(arr);
        for(var i = 1;  i < arr.length;i++){
            if (arr[i] >= 'A' && arr[i]  <= 'Z'){
                arr[i] = arr[i].toLowerCase();
                arr.splice(i,0,' ');
            }
        }
        //alert(arr);
        var newStr = arr.join('');
    
        //alert(newStr);
       return newStr;
    }
    var res = wordTransfer('helloMyWorld')
    document.write(res);
    
    ```

10. ```js
    å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ç»ƒä¹ ï¼š
    
    çŸ­ä¿¡éªŒè¯ç ï¼š éšæœºç”Ÿæˆä¸€ä¸ªnä½çš„ç”±0-9æ•°å­—ç»„æˆçš„çŸ­ä¿¡éªŒè¯ç ã€‚
    function NumberCode(n){
        // parameter n is the digital numbers of the verifcation code;
        // input : 6 
        // output : 564561  / 554897 / ....
        // most used in SMS verify
        var arr = new Array(n);
        for(var i = 0; i < arr.length;i++){
            var temp = parseInt(10 * Math.random());
            arr[i] = temp;
        }
        var str = arr.join('');
        return str;
    }
    
    alert(NumberCode(6));
    
    
    éšæœºéªŒè¯ç ç”Ÿæˆï¼š éšæœºç”Ÿæˆä¸€ä¸ªnä½çš„ç”±a-zå’ŒA-Zä»¥åŠ0-9ç»„æˆçš„éªŒè¯ç ã€‚
    
    function verifyCode(n){
        // parameter n is the digital numbers of the verifcation code;
        // input : 6 
        // output : 5A4c6z  / 5w4R9q / ....
       // a - z ASCII  65 - 90
       // A - Z ASCII  97 - 122
       // 0 - 9  ASCII 0 - 9
       var arr = new Array(n);
       for(var i = 0 ; i < n; i++){
           var temp =  parseInt((Math.random() * 123));
           if(temp >= 0 && temp <= 9){
               arr[i] = temp;
           }else if(temp <= 90 && temp >= 65){
               arr[i] = String.fromCharCode(temp);
           }else if(temp >= 97 && temp <= 122){
               arr[i] = String.fromCharCode(temp);
           }else{
               i = i - 1;
               //i--;
               //omit this time, i goes back to last value, restart this time's pick.
           }
       }
    //    alert(arr);
       var str = arr.join('');
       return str;
    }
    
    alert(verifyCode(6));
    ```

12. ```js
     å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ç»ƒä¹ ï¼š
     å°†å­—ç¬¦ä¸² æŒ‰ç…§å•è¯è¿›è¡Œé€†åºï¼Œç©ºæ ¼ä½œä¸ºåˆ’åˆ†å•è¯çš„å”¯ä¸€æ¡ä»¶ã€‚
     input : Welcome  to Beijing
     Output : Beijing to Welcome
     
     function reverseStr(str){
         var arr =  str.split(' ');
         //[welcome,to,beijing]
         var newArr  = arr.reverse();
         //[beijing,to,welcome]
         var newStr = newArr.join(' ');
         return newStr;
     }
     
     alert(reverseStr('welcome to beijing'));
    ```

13. ```js
     å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ç»ƒä¹ ï¼š
     inputï¼š ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°ç»„ï¼Œèµ·å§‹å…ƒç´ å’Œä¸ªæ•° éƒ½æœªçŸ¥
     outoutï¼š ä¸€ä¸ªæ–°ç”Ÿæˆçš„æ•°ç»„ï¼Œç”±åŸæ•°ç»„çš„å…ƒç´ æ­£åºååºæ‹¼æ¥è€Œæˆã€‚
     e.g.
     input : [one, two, three]
     output: [one , two, three, three, two ,one]
     
     function duplicateArr(arr){
         var arr1 = arr.concat().reverse();
         var newArr = arr.concat(arr1);
         return newArr;
       //è¿™é¢˜å°±æ˜¯è€ƒå¯Ÿ arrayå¼•ç”¨æ•°æ®ç±»å‹çš„ æ€§è´¨ã€‚
     }

14. ```js
     å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ç»ƒä¹ ï¼š
     å·²çŸ¥ä¸€ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²å¯¹è±¡ä¸­ï¼Œè‹±è¯­å•è¯ç”¨å„ç§éå­—æ¯å­—ç¬¦åˆ†éš”ï¼Œç»Ÿè®¡å•è¯ä¸ªæ•°ã€‚
     input: "Yes, she*is&my@love"
     output: 5
     
     //è§„å¾‹ï¼š å½“å‰é¢ä¸€ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦æ˜¯å­—æ¯ï¼Œè€Œåé¢ä¸€ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦æ˜¯éå­—æ¯æ—¶å€™ï¼Œå‰é¢å°±ä¼šæœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªå•è¯ã€‚
     
     function isWord(str){
       if(str >= 'a' && str <= 'z' || str >= 'A' && str <= 'Z' ){
          return true;
          }
       
       return false;
     }
     
     function countWordNumber(str){
       var count = 0;
       for(var i = 0 ; i <  str.length -1 ; i++){
         if(isWord(str[i] && !isWord(str[i+1])  ){
            count++;
            }
       
       return count;
     }
     alert(countWordNumber('"Yes, she*is&my@love"'));
    ```

15. ```js
     å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ç»ƒä¹ ï¼š
     å®ç°ä¸€ä¸ªå‡½æ•°ï¼ŒæŸ¥æ‰¾å­ä¸²å‡ºç°çš„æ¬¡æ•°ï¼Œè¿”å›å­—ç¬¦ä¸²strä¸­å‡ºç°substringçš„æ¬¡æ•°ã€‚
     input: 'abcabcabc' , 'abc'
     output: 3
     
     //è§„å¾‹ï¼š  ç”¨ split åˆ†éš” substringï¼Œå¾—åˆ°çš„æ•°ç»„ç”±ç©ºç™½ç»„æˆï¼Œæ•°ç»„çš„ä¸ªæ•°-1ï¼Œå°±æ˜¯substringçš„ä¸ªæ•°ã€‚(å› ä¸ºç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªåŒ¹é…çš„abcå¼€å¤´ å’Œ æœ€åä¸€ä¸ªåŒ¹é…çš„abcæœ«å°¾çš„ç©ºæ ¼ä¹Ÿç®—)
     split(''):
     			1ä¸ªabcï¼Œåˆ†æˆa,b,c ä¸‰ä¸ªï¼Œ splitå‡ºæ¥æ•°ç»„é•¿åº¦ä¸º3ï¼Œé‚£æœ‰å‡ ä¸ª''å‘¢ï¼Ÿæ•°ä¸€ä¸‹ï¼Œæ˜¯4ä¸ªã€‚
     split('abc')
            1ä¸ªabc   2ä¸ªç©ºï¼ˆä¹Ÿå°±æ˜¯arré•¿åº¦ï¼‰
            2ä¸ªabc   3ä¸ªç©º
            3ä¸ªabc   4ä¸ªç©º
            nä¸ªabc   n+1ä¸ªç©º
            æ‰€ä»¥ nä¸ªabc  = arr.length - 1
     //       æ±‚index ç”¨ indexofå’Œ search
     function countSubStr(supStr,subStr){
         //input abcabcabc  abc
         //output 3
         var arr = supStr.split(subStr);
         // alert(arr);
         return arr.length - 1;
     }
     
     alert(countSubStr('abcabcabcabca1bc2abc','abc'));
    ```

16. ```js
     å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ç»ƒä¹ ï¼š
     å·²çŸ¥ç”¨æˆ·ååªèƒ½æœ‰æ•°å­—å­—æ¯ä¸‹åˆ’çº¿ç»„æˆï¼Œåˆ¤æ–­é‚®ç®±æ˜¯å¦ç¬¦åˆæ ¼å¼ã€‚
     e.g.  1212_fxy@gmail.com true
     			$sada@gmail.com false
     			dnadas@gasasa.comp false
     
     function mailCheck(str){
         // fxy456_0_654@gmail.com
         var index = str.indexOf('@');
         // alert(index);
         //4 
         if(index == -1){
             return false;
         }
         var endStr = str.substring(str.length-4 ,str.length);
         // alert(endStr);
         if(endStr != '.com'){
         return false;
         }
     
         var startStr = str.substring(0, index);
         for( i = 0 ; i < startStr.length; i++){
             if ( containIllegalChar(startStr[i])){
                 return false;
             }
             }
         return true;
         }
     
     
     function containIllegalChar(str){
         if( str <= 'Z' && str >= 'A' || str <='z' && str >= 'a' || str <=9 && str >= 0 || str == '_'){
             return false;
         }
         return true;
     }
     //å°bugï¼š æ— æ³•åˆ¤æ–­ fxy@4560654@gmail.com æ˜¯å¦åˆæ³•ã€‚
     //åšæ³•ï¼š åšä¸€ä¸ªcountï¼Œcountåœ¨stré‡Œé¢'@'çš„ä¸ªæ•°ï¼Œä¸ç­‰äº1çš„éƒ½ä¸ºfalseã€‚
     //ç„¶å @æ‰€åœ¨çš„indexä¹‹å‰åˆ¤æ–­æ˜¯å¦æ˜¯åˆæ³•å­—ç¬¦ã€‚  ä»@çš„indexå¾€åï¼Œåˆ° .comçš„index å†åˆ¤æ–­ä¸€æ¬¡ã€‚ä¹Ÿå°±æ˜¯ åˆ° arr[str.length-4]è¿™ä¸€ä½ã€‚
     //æœ€ååˆ¤æ–­æœ€åå››ä½ æ˜¯ä¸æ˜¯.comå°±å¯ä»¥äº†ã€‚
     
     
     alert(mailCheck('sadadasdasdasdasda.com')); //false
     alert(mailCheck('ssdsada@gmail.comp')); //false
     alert(mailCheck('$sada@gmail.com'));//false
     alert(mailCheck('sada@gmail.com'));//true
     
     //è¿™é‡Œæˆ‘æƒ³é¢å¤–è°ˆä¸€è°ˆ if å’Œif-elseçš„åŒºåˆ«ã€‚
     if( æ¡ä»¶ ){
       
     }
     if( æ¡ä»¶ ){
       
     }
     è¿™æ ·å†™çš„è¯ï¼Œä¸¤ä¸ªifæ²¡æœ‰äº’è¡¥çš„å…³ç³»ï¼Œä»–ä»¬åˆ¤æ–­çš„ æ ·æœ¬æ€»é‡äº’ä¸å½±å“ï¼Œæ¯”å¦‚éƒ½æ˜¯æ•°ç»„ã€‚
     
     ä½†æ˜¯å¦‚æœå†™ï¼š
     if( tiaojian ){
       
     }else{
     	exe2;  
     }

17. ```js
     æ•æ„Ÿè¯å±è”½åŠŸèƒ½ï¼š
     è¾¾åˆ°æ•ˆæœï¼š åœ¨è¾“å…¥æ¡†ä¸­è¾“å…¥ä¸€ä¸²å­—ï¼Œç‚¹å‡»æäº¤åï¼Œæ˜¾ç¤ºåœ¨ä¸‹æ–¹çš„èŠå¤©æ¡†ä¸­ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”è¾“å…¥æ¡†çš„å­—æ¶ˆå¤±ã€‚èŠå¤©æ¡†ä¸­æ˜¾ç¤ºåˆšåˆšå‘é€çš„å†…å®¹ï¼Œä½†æ˜¯å±è”½æ‰äº† æ•æ„Ÿè¯ã€‚

         alert('your mom  has been clean');
         document.getElementById('inputTxt').value ='';
     }
     
     function submitContext(){
         var tranTxt = document.getElementById('inputTxt').value;
         var arr = [/wocao/ig,/nimabi/ig,/wori/ig];
         for(var i = 0; i < arr.length;i++){
             tranTxt = tranTxt.replace(arr[i],'*');
         }
         
            document.getElementById('chatBox').innerHTML =  document.getElementById('chatBox').innerHTML + tranTxt;
     
         document.getElementById('inputTxt').value = '';
     }

     ```js
     function usernameCheck(){
         var str = document.getElementById('usernameInput').value;
         if(str.length > 18 ||  str.length < 6){
             document.getElementById('usernameCheckInfo').innerHTML = 'length must be 8-18';
         }else if(str[0] <= '9' && str[0] >= '0'){
             document.getElementById('usernameCheckInfo').innerHTML = 'the first letter can not be a number';
         }else  if(containIllegalChar(str)){
             document.getElementById('usernameCheckInfo').innerHTML = 'can only contain 0-9 a-Z and _';
           //containIllegalChar use a str loop to check every char in the str if contain a unwanted char.
           // for (var i in str){
           // if containIllegal(str[i])
           // return true
         }
         }else{
             document.getElementById('usernameCheckInfo').innerHTML = 'congrats, you can use this username';
         }
     }

## æ—¥æœŸå¯¹è±¡

1. ```js

5. ```js
    è®¡ç®—2ä¸ªæ—¥æœŸä¹‹é—´ç›¸è·å¤šå°‘å¤©ã€‚
    
    Input : date1 ,date2
    Output: XX days;
    
    function countDays( date1,date2){
      	// å–çš„ä»–ä»¬2ä¸ªæ—¥æœŸç›¸å½“äº1970å¹´çš„æ¯«ç§’å·®ã€‚
     date1 å’Œ date2ç›®å‰æ˜¯ å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬è¦æŠŠä»– å®ä¾‹åŒ–ä¸º dateå¯¹è±¡çš„å®ä¾‹ï¼š
        var d1 = new Date(date1);
        var d2 = new Date(date2);
        var dd1 = d1.getTime();
        var dd2 = d2.getTime();
        var seconds = Math.abs(dd1 - dd2)
        var days = parseInt(seconds /1000/3600/24);
    
        return days;
    }
    ```

4. ```js
    js -åŸºç¡€ç‰ˆ-
      
    window.onload = function(){
        var i = 0;
        var temp = 0;
        // var arr = [];
        temp = setInterval(function(){
            var date = new Date;
            $('timer').innerHTML = date;
        } , 100);
    
        function $( id ){
            return document.getElementById(id);
        }
    
        function changeNumber(num){
            if(num < 10){
                return '0'+num;
            }else if (num >= 10){
                return num;
            }else{
                return 0;
            }
        }
    
    
        $('start').onclick = function(){
            temp = setInterval(function(){
                i++;
                showTimer(i);
            } , 200);
            // arr.push(temp);
            $('start').setAttribute('disabled','disabled');
            $('pause').removeAttribute('disabled');
        };
    
        $('pause').setAttribute('disabled','disabled');
    	
        $('pause').onclick = function(){
            // for(i in arr){
            //     clearInterval(arr[i]);
            // };
            clearInterval(temp);
            $('start').removeAttribute('disabled');
            $('pause').setAttribute('disabled','disabled');
            
        };
    
        function showTimer(i){
            //set hours;
            $('readMeterHours').innerHTML = changeNumber(parseInt(i / 3600));
            //set mins;
            $('readMeterMins').innerHTML = 
            changeNumber(parseInt((i /60)% 60));
            //set seconds;
            $('readMeterSeconds').innerHTML = 
            changeNumber(i % 60);
        }
    
        $('restart').onclick = function(){
            $('pause').setAttribute('disabled','disabled');
            $('start').removeAttribute('disabled');
            i = 0;
            showTimer(i);
        };
    };
    
    
    js---è¿›é˜¶ç‰ˆ-- æš‚åœå¼€å§‹æŒ‰é’®æ•´åˆèµ·æ¥--
    $('restart').onclick = function(){

            $('start').removeAttribute('disabled');
            i = 0;
            showTimer(i);
        };
    
        // $('startAndPause').innerHTML = 'ssss';
        // when click first time, start changed to pause
        //click again ,pause will change to start;
        $('startAndPause').onclick = function(){
            var prompt = $('startAndPause').innerHTML;
            // get current value is start or pause;
            if(prompt == 'å¼€å§‹'){     
                 $('startAndPause').innerHTML = 'æš‚åœ';
                 //start a timer;
                 i = 0 ;
                 temp = setInterval(function (){
                    i++;
                    showTimer(i);
                 },1000);
            }else if(prompt == 'æš‚åœ'){
                 $('startAndPause').innerHTML = 'å¼€å§‹';
                 //pause this timer;
                 clearInterval(temp);
            };

      open('www.baidu.com','_blank','left:100,top:200,scrollbar:yes');
      //nameå¡«_blank,é‚£ç‚¹å‡»åï¼Œç”Ÿæˆæ–°é¡µé¢è·³è½¬æˆbaiduã€‚æœ‰ç‚¹åƒaæ ‡ç­¾é‡Œé¢çš„targetå±æ€§ã€‚
      ä½†æ˜¯åŒºåˆ«æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªæ˜¯aæ ‡ç­¾è§¦å‘ï¼Œè¿™é‡Œæ˜¯ç‚¹å‡»buttonè§¦å‘ã€‚
      open('','xxxx','left:100,top:200,scrollbar:yes');
      //urlä¸å¡«ï¼Œé‚£å°±æ˜¯ç”Ÿæˆç©ºç™½é¡µï¼Œè¯¥çª—å£ nameè®¾ç½®ä¸ºxxxçš„è¯ï¼Œç›¸å½“äºæŠŠurlåœ°å€ä¸è¿™ä¸ªè¯¥çª—å£çš„nameç»‘å®šï¼Œåé¢ä»»ä½•å…³äºxxxçš„æ“ä½œï¼Œéƒ½ä¼šé”å®šåˆ°è¿™ä¸ªå«xxxçš„çª—å£æ¥æ“ä½œï¼Œæ¯”å¦‚æ“ä½œurlã€‚
      
    }
      
      
    Parameter	Description
    
    *URL	//ç»™æ–°å»ºçª—å£è®¾ç½®url
    Optional. 
    Specifies the URL of the page to open. If no URL is specified, a new window/tab with about:blank is opened
    
    *name	 //ç»™æ–°å»ºçª—å£èµ·åå­—
    Optional. 
    Specifies the target attribute or the name of the window. The following values are supported:
    
    _blank - URL is loaded into a new window, or tab. This is default
    _parent - URL is loaded into the parent frame
    _self - URL replaces the current page
    _top - URL replaces any framesets that may be loaded
    name - The name of the window (Note: the name does not specify the title of the new window)
    
    *specs	//ç»™æ–°å»ºçª—å£è®¾ç½®æ ·å¼
    Optional. 
    A comma-separated list of items, no whitespaces. The following values are supported:
    
    channelmode=yes|no|1|0	Whether or not to display the window in theater mode. Default is no. IE only
    directories=yes|no|1|0	Obsolete. Whether or not to add directory buttons. Default is yes. IE only
    fullscreen=yes|no|1|0	Whether or not to display the browser in full-screen mode. Default is no. A window in full-screen mode must also be in theater mode. IE only
    height=pixels	The height of the window. Min. value is 100
    left=pixels	The left position of the window. Negative values not allowed
    location=yes|no|1|0	Whether or not to display the address field. Opera only
    menubar=yes|no|1|0	Whether or not to display the menu bar
    resizable=yes|no|1|0	Whether or not the window is resizable. IE only
    scrollbars=yes|no|1|0	Whether or not to display scroll bars. IE, Firefox & Opera only
    status=yes|no|1|0	Whether or not to add a status bar
    titlebar=yes|no|1|0	Whether or not to display the title bar. Ignored unless the calling application is an HTML Application or a trusted dialog box
    toolbar=yes|no|1|0	Whether or not to display the browser toolbar. IE and Firefox only
    top=pixels	The top position of the window. Negative values not allowed
    width=pixels	The width of the window. Min. value is 100
    
    *replace	
    Optional. 
    Specifies whether the URL creates a new entry or replaces the current entry in the history list. 
    The following values are supported:
    
    true - URL replaces the current document in the history list
    false - URL creates a new entry in the history list
    ```

5. ```js
    ç”±äºIE8ä¸å…¼å®¹getClassNameæ–¹æ³•ã€‚
    
    æˆ‘ä»¬å¦‚ä½•è‡ªå®šä¹‰å®ç° node.getElementsByClassName( );
    
    ä¹Ÿå°±æ˜¯ä¸ç”¨å®˜æ–¹çš„ node.getElementsByClassName( );å¦‚ä½•æ˜¯ç”¨åŸç”Ÿå®ç° ä¸€æ ·çš„åŠŸèƒ½ï¼š
    
       function getEleByClassName(node,classStr){
            //input: node name ; class name
            //output node.getElementsByClassName('class')
           // but you can not use node.getElementsByClassName('class')
    
           var oTag = node.getElementsByTagName('*');
           //æœ€å…³é”®çš„ä¸€ç‚¹ï¼Œå°±æ˜¯è¿™é‡Œï¼šåˆ©ç”¨tagå†™*çš„è¯å¯ä»¥å–åˆ°nodeä¸‹é¢çš„æ‰€æœ‰èŠ‚ç‚¹ã€‚
           var arr = [];
           //å­˜æ”¾ç¬¦åˆæ¡ä»¶çš„èŠ‚ç‚¹
           for(var i = 0 ; i < oTag.length;i++){
               if(oTag[i].className == classStr){
                   arr.push(oTag[i]);
               }
           }
           return arr;
        }
    
        alert(getEleByClassName($('eleTest'),'btn').length);

6. ```js
    å¦‚ä½•è·å–å½“å‰æœ‰æ•ˆæ ·å¼ï¼š
    
    1. node.style.xxx åªèƒ½å®šä½åˆ° nodeå…ƒç´ èŠ‚ç‚¹çš„å†…è”æ ·å¼ã€‚å¦‚æœcssæ˜¯å¤–éƒ¨çš„ï¼Œæˆ–è€…æ˜¯å¤´éƒ¨çš„ï¼Œå°±ä¸å¯ä»¥é€šè¿‡style.xxxç›´æ¥æŸ¥è¯¢åˆ°çš„ã€‚è€Œä¸”ä¸€èˆ¬éƒ½æ˜¯å¤–é“¾æ ·å¼ã€‚

    function getCssStyle(node , style){
      if(node.currentStyle){
         			return node.currentStyle[style];
         }else{
        			return getComputedStyle(node,null)[style];
      }
    }
    
    æˆ‘æƒ³æŸ¥è¯¢ä¸€ä¸ªnodeçš„æœ‰æ•ˆæ ·å¼çš„è¯ï¼š
